 Strange as it may sound, but the indo-tibetan Border Police (ITBP) jawans have started teaching in local schools for the last one and a half years in Kondagaon district of Chhattisgarh, which is battling Naxalite violence
 Sasneh Halbi has also learned to speak
 kondagaanv ke zyada samay nahin hua jab hadeli or aise kai gaanvon ke paas sthapit itibipi camp main tainaat javaanon ne sthaneey skulon ke bacchon ko ganit vigyaan or anya vishyon main padhaane kaa bidaa uthaaya tha
 Whenever the soldiers were on leave from their work, they used to go to these schools as teachers
 ab bacchon ko yah avasar mila he ki ve apni maatrubhaasha sikhaane ke liye shikshak kii bhoomika main dikhne lage hai
 The ITBP camp was opened about a year and a half ago in Hadeli, a heavily Naxal-affected area adjoining Abujhmad
 yahaan kii sthaneey boli halbi javaanon ke liye ek samasya thi or bolchaal ke liye javaanon ko graminon kii madad leni padati thi
 Due to this linguistic barrier, they were unable to communicate among themselves
 duurastha ilaake main jab bhi jawan abhiyaanon ke baad gaanv ke skulon main jate the to sthaneey skulon main shikshakon kii kami ke kaaran bacchon ko unki padhai main madad bhi karne lage
 Gradually the mutual trust of the villagers and the ITBP jawans of the school children increased so much that the children themselves started teaching the jawans to speak and write halbi
 vidhyalay main praathmik or madhyamik kakshaon main kul 85 chaatr chatraayen adhyayanrat hai
 In this area, ITBP not only pioneered education but also started providing clean water to the surrounding areas and giving them medicines on minor diseases
 javaanon kii is pahal se is kshetra main schuli bacchon kaa bhavishya sanvaarane kii ek sakaaratmak pahal to ho hi rahi he lekin saath hi jawan bhashaa ke madhyam se ilaake ko behatar samajhane main bhi kaamyaab rahe hai
 Due to this, not only has the force reconciled with the local people, but there has also been a huge decrease in Naxalite activities
 aasapaas ke kshetron se saikadon naksaliyon ne aatmasamarpan kar diya he

 In the wake of mass media involvement in school education since 2011 and the knocking of foreign universities in the country, the media school of IP University has taken its back
 bhavi chunautiyon se nipatane kii kii kya ranneeti ho sakati he, bataa rahe hai ypi uniwarsity ke professor incharge chandrakant prasad singh
 Question- What will be the impact on media schools with the arrival of foreign universities in India? Answer - Foreign universities will bring experience, technology and expertise with them, in that case the universities present in the country will also have to improve the level of education significantly and link education with industry
 prashn- aapke hisaab se yah sudhaar kya ho sakate hai? uttar- dekhie, media kii vishvavidhyalayan shiksha kii sabase badi kamajori yah bataaya ja rahaa he ki vah bazaronmukh nahin he
 This is the reason why the industry shows less eagerness towards the children who have come to train from universities
 yah sudhaar do-tarafa karnaa hoga
 The first is that the course taught in media schools will have to be changed extensively, so that it can meet the needs of society and the market, and second it must be strategic
 prashn- ranneeti sudhaar se aapkaa kya matlab he? uttar- ranneetik kehane kaa matlab yah he ki sudhaar sthaneey jaruraton, vaishvik chunautiyon or maukey ke hisaab se hona chahie
 Look at the ancient education system of India
 behatar shiksha vyavastha kaa hamaara itihaas purana he
 We had the world famous Nalanda University, where people from all over the world used to come for education, but over time our education system declined and at the same time our development was also disrupted
 aaj jab ham phir se vikaas ke path par chal pade hai, to jaruri he ki ham apni shiksha vyavastha ko chust-durust karen or samay ke hisaab se parivartit karen, taaki hamaara vikascram jari rahe, or vishwa guru kii jo bharat kii puraani chhavi thi vah praapt kiya ja sake
 Question: From next year, media is being added as a subject in schools too
 aise main bhavi jaruraton ko lekar aapke paas kya rodmap he? uttar- 2011 se skulon main 11veen or 12veen kaksha main media ko bhi ek vishay ke rup main jode jane kaa sidhaa matlab yah he ki 2013-14 se kareeb 7 lakh bachche uniwarsity str par is vishay main graduate karnaa chahenge, aise main kam se kam 40 hajaar college shikshakon kii jarurat hogi
 Therefore, it would be prudent to prepare for the challenges ahead in time and also to have a vision
 prashn- aap bharat main media skool kaa kya bhavishya dekhte hai? uttar- media kshetra kii vikaas dar 12 se 14 fisadi salanaa he, jo telecom sector ke baad sabase zyada he, isliye isko darkinar nahin kiya ja saktaa
 In fact, the meaning of education in media has mostly been taken from journalism, while the non-journalistic field is equally important, which includes advertising and mass communication, animation, media management, etc
 media kaa hi ek vishay communication kii padhai management ke chaatr bhi ek vishay ke rup main karte hai
 In the coming time, it will expand further and as a personality development it will be included in all professional courses
 isliye mere hisaab se to media skool kaa bhavishya ujjwal he
 Question- But you will agree that journalism is also an important field and an emerging industry
 to aise main industry se vishvavidhyalay kii duuri ko aap kaise paatenge? uttar- aap bilkul sahi kah rahe hai or main bhi isse puraa ittefaq rakhata hum
 Therefore, we have created a cell to connect our media school to the industry, which will have the best professionals associated with the industry, along with university teachers
 jo na sirf yahaan ke vidhyaarthiyon ke pradarshan ko jaanchenge, balki industry kii jaruraton ke hisaab se course main tabdili bhi suzaayenge
 Question- The biggest drawback of higher education in India has been that we are not giving too much emphasis on research
 ypi kaa media skool is ore kya kadam uthaa rahaa he? uttar- hamaare kulapati professor dike bandopadhyaay research ko bahut adhik mahatv dete hai or ek duuradrashtaa vyakti hai
 That is why we have decided to increase media research soon
 yahi kaaran he ki aane vaale 5-6 maheene main jansanchaar main piechdi kii shuruyaat ham karne ja rahe hai, jisaki manjuuri mil chuki he
 Not only this, we have also decided to give extensive emphasis on research at the Masters level
 media main masters kar rahe vidhyaarthiyon ko teen shodh patr jamaa karne honge, jinamein se do chote honge or ek vistrut adhyayan hoga
 The direct benefit of this will be that the trend of students will move towards research and development of many media models will be possible in the country
